gdal-doc in epel-7

This page displays detail informations of the gdal-doc package. You might want go back to the main page of gdal-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2017-12-21 Orion Poplawski - 1.11.4-3 - Rebuild again for new armadillo
2017-12-11 Mukundan Ragavan - 1.11.4-2 - rebuild for armadillo
2016-02-14 Volker Froehlich - 1.11.4-1 - New release
2016-02-04 Volker Froehlich - 1.11.3-1 - New release - Solve BZ #1271906 (Build iso8211 and s57 utilities) - Support openjpeg2
2015-12-10 Dan Horák - 1.11.2-2 - workaround libtool bug in RHEL 7.2 (rhbz#1287191)
2015-07-07 Volker Fröhlich - 1.11.2-1 - New release - Rebuild for g2clib (bz 1203582) - Update gdal-config for aarch64 and ppc64le (bz 1227642)
2014-11-18 Volker Fröhlich - 1.11.1-1 - New release - Correct test suite source URL
2014-06-07 Fedora Release Engineering - 1.11.0-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_21_Mass_Rebuild
2014-04-25 Volker Fröhlich - 1.11.0-1 - New upstream release - Remove libgcj as BR, as it no longer exists in F21 - Re-enable ogdi and spatialite where possible - Adapt Python-BR to python2-devel - Obsolete Ruby bindings, due to the suggestion of Even Rouault - Preserve timestamp of Fedora README file - Explicitly create HTML documentation with Doxygen - Make test execution conditional - Truncate changelog
2014-04-24 Vít Ondruch - 1.10.1-7 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/Ruby_2.1
